                      - generic [ref=f27e46]:
                        - generic [ref=f27e52]:
                          - heading "Frames Practice" [level=1] [ref=f27e55]
                          - article [ref=f27e56]:
                            - generic [ref=f27e57]:
                              - generic [ref=f27e58]: "This page is used for practicing iframes in web automation. We have three types of frames in web applications, those are:"
                              - list [ref=f27e60]:
                                - listitem [ref=f27e61]:
                                  - text: frame - The
                                  - generic [ref=f27e62]: <frame>
                                  - text: tag was used in HTML 4 to define one particular window (frame) within a
                                  - generic [ref=f27e63]: <frameset>
                                  - text: .
                                - listitem [ref=f27e64]:
                                  - text: frameset - The
                                  - generic [ref=f27e65]: <frameset>
                                  - text: tag was used in HTML 4 to define a frameset.
                                - listitem [ref=f27e66]:
                                  - text: iframe - The
                                  - generic [ref=f27e67]: <iframe>
                                  - text: tag specifies an inline frame. An inline frame is used to embed another document within the current HTML document.
                              - generic [ref=f27e68]: Out of these, frame and frameset were no longer being supported in HTML 5. Below we have three frames to practice.
                              - generic [ref=f27e69]:
                                - generic [ref=f27e70]:
                                  - paragraph [ref=f27e71]

                                            - heading "Frames Practice" [level=1] [ref=f36e59]
                                            - article [ref=f36e60]:
                                              - generic [ref=f36e61]:
                                                - generic [ref=f36e62]: "This page is used for practicing iframes in web automation. We have three types of frames in web applications, those are:"
                                                - list [ref=f36e64]:
                                                  - listitem [ref=f36e65]:
                                                    - text: frame - The
                                                    - generic [ref=f36e66]: <frame>
                                                    - text: tag was used in HTML 4 to define one particular window (frame) within a
                                                    - generic [ref=f36e67]: <frameset>
                                                    - text: .
                                                  - listitem [ref=f36e68]:
                                                    - text: frameset - The
                                                    - generic [ref=f36e69]: <frameset>
                                                    - text: tag was used in HTML 4 to define a frameset.
                                                  - listitem [ref=f36e70]:
                                                    - text: iframe - The
                                                    - generic [ref=f36e71]: <iframe>
                                                    - text: tag specifies an inline frame. An inline frame is used to embed another document within the current HTML document.
                                                - generic [ref=f36e72]: Out of these, frame and frameset were no longer being supported in HTML 5. Below we have three frames to practice.
                                                - generic [ref=f36e73]:
                                                  - generic [ref=f36e74]:
                                                    - paragraph [ref=f36e75]
                                                    - paragraph [ref=f36e76]: This textbox is used for entering the text after switching back from frames.
                                                    - textbox [ref=f36e77]
                                                  - generic [ref=f36e78]:
                                                    - heading "Frame1:" [level=3] [ref=f36e79]
                                                    - iframe [ref=f36e80]: <p>Your browser does not support iframes.</p>:
